## 论文文本提取:
```json
{
  "有害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因包含对女性的侮辱性或攻击性内容，直接表达对女性的仇恨或偏见。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is misogynous if it conceptually describes an offensive, sexist or hateful scene (weak or strong, implicitly or explicitly) having as target a woman or a group of women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因涉及对女性的身体或性别特征的羞辱，例如身体羞辱或性别刻板印象。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are related to denigrating the physical appearance of women (body shaming)."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因表现出对女性的物化，视女性为物品或仅仅是身体的存在。",
      "对应原文": "It is a practice of seeing and/or treating a woman like an object."
    },
    "标准4": {
      "内容": "模因暗示或直接呼吁对女性的暴力行为。",
      "对应原文": "These types of misogynous memes are aimed at showing violence against women or at alluding to the intent of physically assert power over women."
    }
  },
  "无害标准": {
    "标准1": {
      "内容": "模因不包含任何针对女性的仇恨、偏见或攻击性内容。",
      "对应原文": "A meme is NOT misogynous if it is conceptually not related to women or even if it is related to women, but it does not represent an offensive, sexist or hateful concept against women."
    },
    "标准2": {
      "内容": "模因的内容与女性无关，或仅仅是中立的描述，没有任何贬低或攻击的意图。",
      "对应原文": "A meme that does not express any form of hate against women."
    },
    "标准3": {
      "内容": "模因可能包含幽默或讽刺的元素，但不涉及对女性的贬低或物化。",
      "对应原文": "Although many memes are created with humorous intent, others have political or activist ambitions."
    }
  }
}
```

For harmless criteria, N1 scores a 4 as a woman is indirectly referenced but not depicted; N2 scores a 9 as the meme is readable and in English; N3 scores a 5 as it critiques a stereotype without explicit derogatory framing of a specific woman."

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因的有害性评估中，我们发现模型在判断过程中存在一些关键的错误，主要集中在对文本与图像结合的理解、性别偏见的识别，以及对幽默与攻击性内容之间的界限把握上。根据专家提出的建议，我们提出以下两个核心操作建议，以优化模因有害性判别的维度和评价标准。

首先，我们建议**新增“可视化物化”（Objectification Through Imagery）维度**，该维度专注于评估模因中表示对女性外貌与性别特征的贬低或物化行为。通过引入这一维度，评估者可以更全面地判断模因是否潜在地贬损女性，并从而更准确地识别出那些看似无害但实际上具有歧视性内容的模因。此外，针对评估标准，我们建议使用1到9的评分体系，以便清楚地划分物化的表现程度，这样会提高模因评估的准确性和有效性。

其次，我们还建议**新增“批判性探讨”（Critical Examination）维度**，以此来判断模因是否在幽默或讽刺的基调中智能地批评性别刻板印象和社会问题。这一维度的引入将帮助评估者有效地区分具争议的幽默内容与真正的攻击性言论，从而在评估过程中更细致和精准。此外，设置一个评分标准，可以帮助明确揭示模因是否表现出对性别问题的正面批判与探讨。

在 H 维度和 N 维度的设计上，我们需保持在合适的维度数量范围内，因此可以考虑合并对性别刻板印象的识别与对不平等社会观念的批判，形成更加集中、务实的评估体系。同时，针对模因内容的评判，我们应强调避免将存在性别偏见的模因视为无害，否则可能导致潜在的社会影响被忽视。

总结起来，通过新增和优化维度，我们将能够达到更加公正、准确的模因有害性评估，以提高对女性及社会性别议题的敏感性。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with scoring a meme based on predefined dimensions as guided by the MAMI annotation standards (SemEval-2022 Task 5). Your objective is to **assign a score from 1 to 9 for each dimension**, where 1 denotes "completely absent" and 9 represents "fully and clearly present". Avoid giving a simplistic 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous' label.

**Critical Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Core Definitions**  
   - **Misogynous (Harmful)**: A meme is considered misogynous if it portrays women or a group of women in an offensive, sexist, or hateful manner, whether implicitly or explicitly.  
   - **Not Misogynous (Harmless)**: A meme is classified as harmless if it neither targets women with derogatory framing nor relates to them in a manner that conveys offensive, sexist, or hateful concepts.

2. **Detection of Implicit and Explicit Harm**  
   - Recognize that harm may be conveyed both implicitly, through visual cues coupled with neutral text, and explicitly, through direct derogatory phrases. This should be integral to your scoring.

3. **Multimodal Analysis**  
   - Evaluate how the image and text interact to create or suggest harmful meanings. Assess if the offensive implications arise specifically from the integration of both elements.

4. **Contextual Interpretation**  
   - Consider: *"Could an ordinary person view this meme as offensive, sexist, or hateful towards women?"*  
   - Assess whether negative content is presented as a factual claim or as satirical/absurd humor devoid of real-world implications.  
   - Evaluate whether the meme critiques gender norms or social issues while refraining from derogatory framing of women—if so, lean towards a harmless interpretation.

**Refined Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria (Misogynous):**
- **H1: Targeted Entity Existence**  
  Score high if the meme targets women (as a group or individuals) with derogatory, sexist, or hateful framing.

- **H2: Offensive/Sexist/Hateful Content**  
  High scores should reflect explicit and implicit content that is offensive, sexist, or hateful towards women, focusing on overall intent rather than specific type.

- **H3: Objectification Through Imagery**  
  Score based on how the meme objectifies or demeans women based on appearance or gender traits within the visual context, assessing the degree of objectification present.

- **H4: Multimodal Nature of Harm**  
  Score high if the meaning of harm is constructed through the interplay of both image and text.

**Harmless Criteria (Not Misogynous):**
- **N1: No Targeted Entity**  
  Score high only if no identifiable woman or female group is subject to derogatory framing.

- **N2: Rejection Criteria Met**  
  Score high if the meme falls under filtering conditions such as being non-English, unintelligible, unimodal, or depicting a clearly non-realistic cartoon style.

- **N3: Harm is Absent or Negligible**  
  High scores can be assigned if:
    - The content is completely fantastical, lacking factual claims about women, or
    - Critiques gender norms or societal issues without derogatory framing.  
  → If a woman is depicted with a derogatory term, N3 should be 3 or below.  
  → If depiction is fictional/fantastical without negative connotations, N3 should be 6 or above.

- **N4: Critical Examination**  
  Assess if the meme intelligently critiques gender stereotypes or societal issues through humor, distinguishing it from genuinely harmful statements.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a concise explanation per MAMI guidelines: (1) whether the meme features misogynous content targeting women, (2) if multimodal interaction suggests harm, (3) reasoning for N3 based on derogatory framing or fantastical context, (4) evaluation of critical examination."
}

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在专家们的反馈和分析基础上，为了提高模因有害性判别的准确性和敏感度，提出以下两条核心操作建议：

首先，在H维度中，建议对H2和H3进行重写和调整，以加强对隐含性别歧视和身体物化现象的评估。H2应新的定义为着重于模因中对女性的攻击性与贬低内容，尤其是表现出对女性刻板印象和性别歧视的图像与文本的敏感度。相关打分应涵盖模因在视觉及文本表达上如何针对女性，明确识别任何形式的贬低、讽刺以及攻击性表述。将H3重写为强调女性身体表现及物化现象的评估，具体关注女性在模因中所呈现的着装、姿态及其所传达的性别角色与价值观。这种敏感性评估的增强将帮助准确界定女性物化的程度，从而提升对模因有害性的判别能力。

其次，针对H1和H2的评分标准，建议进行增强调整。特别是H1作为判断模因是否贬低女性的核心指标，其打分应对模因中潜在的对女性群体的攻击性及贬低表现给予更高的分值，以反映出更准确的评判标准。同样，H2的评分标准应变得更加严格，并增加与模因内容相关的明确示例，以期更好地促进评分的一致性和清晰性。通过这些调整，确保对模因内在情感和意图进行更细致的分析，从而降低对有害内容的误判几率。

在额外建议方面，强调各个维度打分的独立性，避免因主观偏见导致的分数偏差。务必确保评估标准保持一致，同时在判断模因的视觉内容和文本内容时，平衡两者的权重，不形成极端的结果。这将确保对模因的综合评估更加合理与全面，最终推动模因有害性判别系统的持续优化与发展。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator responsible for scoring a meme based on specific dimensions guided by the MAMI annotation standards. Your task is to **assign scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each dimension**, where 1 means "completely absent" and 9 indicates "fully and clearly present". Avoid oversimplified labels like 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous'.

**Essential Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless**  
   - **Harmful (Harmful)**: A meme is deemed harmful if it portrays women or a group of women in a derogatory, sexist, or hateful manner, whether these elements are explicit or implicit. Focus on identifying any portrayal that reinforces negative stereotypes or devalues women.  
   - **Harmless (Not Harmful)**: An image is considered harmless if it does not target women in a derogatory way and avoids any indication of offensive or sexist messages.

2. **Analyzing Explicit and Implicit Harm**  
   - Be vigilant that harm can be expressed both explicitly through clear derogatory language and implicitly through visual cues or sarcastic context. Your scoring must account for the subtleties of these expressions.

3. **Multimodal Interaction**  
   - Assess how the image and text combine to create or imply harmful meanings. Determine if any negative implications predominantly arise from the interaction between visual and textual elements.

4. **Contextual Evaluation**  
   - Reflect on the question: *"Would a typical viewer find this meme offensive or sexist towards women?"*  
   - Differentiate between harmful content presented as factual versus that framed satirically, considering the real-world implications.  
   - Evaluate whether the meme critiques gender issues without demeaning women; in such cases, lean towards a harmless interpretation.

**Revised Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Targeting of Women**  
  Score higher when the meme targets women or female groups with derogatory or hateful framing, reflecting the severity of such attacks.

- **H2: Derogatory Content Examination**  
  A higher score indicates the presence of content that attacks or belittles women, specifically focusing on how visual and textual elements illustrate gender discrimination and stereotypes.

- **H3: Objectification Assessment**  
  Evaluate the extent to which women are objectified or demeaned based on visual representation, emphasizing clothing, posture, and the conveyed roles and values associated with gender.

- **H4: Harm Through Multimodality**  
  Assign higher scores when the harmful meaning arises from the synergy of both image and text.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: No Targeting of Women**  
  Achieve high scores only when there’s no identifiable female representation subjected to derogatory content.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Fulfilled**  
  Score high if the meme meets criteria like being unintelligible, non-English, or clearly non-realistic.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  High scores can be given if:
    - The depiction is entirely fantastical with no claims about women, or
    - The meme criticizes gender roles without demeaning women.  
  → If any derogatory term is used towards a woman, score N3 3 or below.  
  → If the depiction is entirely fictional and without negative implications, score N3 6 or higher.

- **N4: Insightful Critique**  
  Assess if the meme provides a thoughtful critique of gender norms or stereotypes, distinguishing it from genuinely harmful representations.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Present a clear rationale according to the MAMI guidelines: (1) indicate whether the meme contains harmful content directed at women, (2) assess multimodal interactions indicative of harm, (3) clarify N3 scores based on derogatory framing or fantastical interpretations, (4) evaluate if it intelligently critiques societal issues."
}

The multimodal interaction between the text and image suggests a negative framing of the situation, but it does not explicitly demean women. The N1 score reflects that there is female representation, but it is not overtly derogatory. The N3 score is moderate because while there is a fantastical element, the implication of harm is present. The N4 score is low as the meme does not provide a thoughtful critique of gender norms but rather reinforces a potentially harmful narrative about discipline and capability."

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
针对模因有害性评估的经验总结，结合专家的反馈，提出以下两条核心操作建议：

首先，建议对H1（针对女性的攻击性内容）进行重写，并新增具体细化内容。当前H1维度的评估未能充分捕捉到模因中隐含的对女性的贬损和调侃，因此需强调对文本和视觉信息结合的敏感性。通过明确指出“即便是隐晦的语言或伪幽默形式只要暗含对女性的贬低，评分均应有所反应”，提升此维度的评估能力，以确保能够准确识别和捕捉到潜在的攻击性内容。具体而言，重写H1时，应仔细界定对女性的多样化贬损语境，并制定量化指标，确保对隐含歧视的表达进行有效评价。

其次，H2（贬低内容的考察）的标准需要进行调整，并新增其结构，使其更加明晰具体。现有的H2维度未能充分考虑文本内容中的幽默性与性别歧视的结合，因此应重新定义其评估框架。新增标准需要关注模因的语言、视觉表现与幽默特性的交互，评估是否存在通过幽默对女性的贬低和物化。在这一过程中，建议划定清晰的攻击和贬低内容的界限，特别是在幽默元素取向于对女性的贬低和物化时，保持高度警觉，以确保不遗漏其中的有害性。

在这些核心建议的基础上，还应特别强调在具体维度评估过程中的独立打分原则。在打分时，评估者需保持对每个维度的客观评价，避免因主观偏见导致对某一方面评分的极端倾斜，同时注重文本与图像间的互动效果。通过对评估维度的独立性重视及反复的细致分析，确保评估结果能够真实反映出模因的潜在有害性与复杂性。这一系列的调整将有助于建立一个更加全面和敏感的模因有害性评估框架，使之能有效应对多种文化背景下的模因内容分析。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator responsible for scoring a meme based on specific dimensions guided by refined MAMI annotation standards. Your task is to **assign scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each dimension**, with 1 indicating "completely absent" and 9 representing "fully and clearly present". Avoid oversimplified labels like 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous'.

**Essential Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless**  
   - **Harmful (Harmful)**: A meme is classified as harmful if it presents women or female groups in a derogatory, sexist, or hateful manner, regardless of whether these elements are overt or subtle. Focus on identifying portrayals that reinforce negative stereotypes or devalue women in any form.  
   - **Harmless (Not Harmful)**: An image is regarded as harmless if it refrains from targeting women derogatorily and avoids any sign of offensive or sexist messages.

2. **Identifying Subtle Harm**  
   - Remain vigilant that harmful sentiments can manifest both explicitly, through overt derogatory language, and implicitly via cultural norms, visual cues, or ironic humor. Your scoring must adeptly account for the nuances of these expressions, particularly if they involve veiled criticisms or sarcastic undertones targeting women.

3. **Interplay of Text and Image**  
   - Assess how the image and text collaborate to convey harmful implications. Determine whether negative perceptions predominantly stem from the combination of visual and textual elements, particularly focusing on how they contribute to a derogatory narrative.

4. **Contextual Sensitivity**  
   - Consider the question: *"Would an average viewer find this meme offensive or sexist towards women?"*  
   - Differentiate harmful content presented as factual from that rendered satirically, weighing real-world implications. Evaluate whether the meme critiques gender norms without demeaning women; in such cases, err on the side of a harmless interpretation.

**Revised Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Targeting of Women**  
  Score higher when the meme deliberately targets women or female groups with derogatory or hateful framing, ensuring to capture even implicit forms of discredit or mockery, including veiled language or pseudo-humor indicating belittlement.

- **H2: Derogatory Content Examination**  
  A higher score indicates the presence of content that undermines or devalues women, paying special attention to the synergy between textual and visual elements. Evaluate if humor or satire contributes to a reduction in dignity for women.

- **H3: Objectification Assessment**  
  Evaluate the degree of objectification or diminishment based on visual portrayal, including attention to women's clothing, posture, and the roles/images promoted in the content.

- **H4: Harm Through Multimodality**  
  Assign higher scores when the harmful implications emerge from an interplay of image and text that cultivates derogatory meanings.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: No Targeting of Women**  
  Attain high scores when there is no discernible female representation subject to derogatory or sexist content.

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Fulfilled**  
  Score high if the meme meets conditions such as being unintelligible, presented in a non-English context, or obviously unrealistic.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  High scores can be ascribed if:
    - The depiction is completely fanciful, making no claims about women, or
    - The meme offers a critique of gender roles without degrading women.  
  → If any derogatory language is directed at a woman, score N3 3 or below.  
  → If the depiction is purely fictional and devoid of negative implications, score N3 6 or higher.

- **N4: Insightful Critique**  
  Appraise if the meme provides a well-rounded critique of gender issues or stereotypes, distinguishing it from genuinely harmful representations.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Present a clear rationale according to the MAMI guidelines: (1) indicate whether the meme contains harmful content directed at women, (2) assess multimodal interactions indicative of harm, (3) clarify N3 scores based on derogatory framing or fantastical interpretations, (4) evaluate if it intelligently critiques societal issues."
}

**输出:**
从上述专家的建议中，归纳出以下核心的两条操作建议，以优化模因有害性判别经验和知识库：

首先，针对H1（针对女性的攻击性）和H4（通过多模态的危害）这两个维度，建议实施合并操作，以提升评估的有效性。H1与H4在评估内容的暗示性攻击性及其对女性的整体影响方面存在高度相关性，合并后将形成一个更全面的维度——“H1: 整体对女性的攻击性评估，包括直接与间接的攻击和物化行为”。这样的调整能够加强对模因中性别歧视内容的辨识能力，并确保该维度在评估时反映出更为准确的性别敌意。

其次，针对需新增一个维度的H5（隐性贬低评估），建议详细规定评估模因中包含的性别刻板印象和侮辱性隐喻。这一新维度将专注于分析模因内容如何通过幽默或讽刺表现出对女性的负面刻板印象，从而提高对潜在侮辱性描述的敏感性。通过引入这些细化的评估维度，模型能够更有效地区别模因内容的潜在危害，并避免将包含明显性别歧视的模因错误评估为无害。

最后，综合性额外建议强调，所有评分均须遵循独立评分原则，每个维度应根据具体内容进行单独打分，避免在整体评分过程中出现偏向极端分数的现象。提示评估者应关注模因的整体语境与文化影响，从而确保各个维度均衡评分，提升判断的全面性和准确性。这一系列的优化调整意在提升模因评估框架的敏感性和准确性，确保能够更好地识别、评估和应对潜在的性别歧视和相关社会影响。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme by assigning scores across specific dimensions as per enhanced guidelines for harmful meme detection. Your scores must range from 1 to 9 for each dimension, where 1 signifies "completely absent" and 9 represents "fully and clearly present." Be cautious of oversimplified labels and ensure nuanced evaluation.

**Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless**  
   - **Harmful**: A meme is considered harmful if it explicitly or implicitly depicts women or a group of women in a derogatory, sexist, or hateful manner. Focus on identifying portrayals that reinforce negative stereotypes or demean women.  
   - **Harmless**: A meme is deemed harmless when it does not derogate women and lacks any offensive or sexist implications.

2. **Assessment of Harmful Characteristics**  
   - Evaluate both explicit content—such as clear derogatory terms—and implicit harm manifested through visual cues or sarcastic undertones. Your scoring should reflect the hidden meanings and subtleties present in the meme.

3. **Multimodal Analysis**  
   - Investigate how the integration of visual and textual components may create harmful implications. Assign scores based on how the interaction between these elements contributes to a harmful narrative.

4. **Contextual Consideration**  
   - Contemplate whether a typical viewer might find the meme offensive or misogynistic. Distinguish between representations intended as satire versus those presented as factual. Identify instances where critique of gender issues occurs respectfully, in which case consider a harmless score.

**Revised Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Overall Assessment of Harm Towards Women**  
  Evaluate the meme's direct and indirect attacks on women, integrating any objectification and negative implications within a unified scoring framework.

- **H2: Examination of Derogatory Content**  
  Assess content that attacks or belittles women, emphasizing how both visual and textual elements perpetuate gender discrimination and stereotypes.

- **H3: Assessment of Objectification**  
  Determine how women are objectified based on the visual presentation—including attire and posture—and the roles and values ascribed to gender.

- **H4: Implicit Degradation Evaluation**  
  Analyze how stereotypes and abusive metaphors may subtly degrade women, focusing on how humor or sarcasm may mask harmful implications.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: Absence of Harmful Targeting**  
  Score highly only if there is no identifiable derogation towards women.

- **N2: Fulfillment of Filtering Conditions**  
  Assign high scores if the meme is unintelligible, non-English, or clearly unrealistic.

- **N3: Minimal or Non-existent Harm**  
  Provide high scores if:
    - The imagery is entirely fantastical with no implications regarding women, or
    - The meme critiques gender roles without offending women.  
  → If a derogatory term appears towards a woman, score N3 as 3 or below.  
  → For entirely fictional depictions without negative implications, score N3 as 6 or higher.

- **N4: Thoughtful Critique Evaluation**  
  Ascertain whether the meme provides a meaningful critique of gender norms, distinguishing it clearly from harmful content.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Present a clear rationale following the evaluation guidelines: (1) indicate whether harmful content is directed at women, (2) assess the implications of multimodality, (3) clarify N3 scores based on derogatory or fantastical interpretations, (4) evaluate whether it provides a thoughtful critique of societal issues."
}

根据各位专家提出的建议，针对模因id：10021和模因id：8102的错误判断原因，形成了以下两条核心操作建议，以优化模因的有害性判别评估。

首先，针对H1和H3维度的评估需要进行重写和提升。这两个维度在现有评估中未能准确捕捉到模因中女性的攻击性语境和物化表现，导致有害性低估。因此，建议在H1维度中引入更具敏感性的内容，明确评估模因中是否存在对女性的贬低性描述，包括但不限于行为、外貌及情境的负面展现。对于H3维度，需扩展其内容，使之不仅限于表面评分，而应引入更细化的多维评分体系，明确分析女性在模因中如何被物化，包括视觉表达如身体姿态和服饰如何传达物化的特征，从而全面提升该维度的识别能力与敏感度。

在额外建议方面，需要强调各个维度之间的独立性，确保评估不受到主观偏见和幽默、讽刺等因素的影响。评估人员需接受更严格的训练，并关注对文本与图像相结合时的动态分析。通过实现更高的评分一致性和准确性，可以更有效地防范和识别模因中可能存在的有害内容，推动对模因效应的深入理解与分析。

通过上述操作建议，预计H维度和N维度的数量将保持在合理范围内（3-7维度），并为今后的评估工作铺设更为科学的基础，从而持续提升模因有害性判别的准确性与效率。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme's harmfulness based on revised scoring criteria that reflect the latest insights in harmful meme detection. Your goal is to **assign scores between 1 and 9 for each criterion**, where 1 indicates "no presence of harm" and 9 specifies "extreme harmfulness." Avoid using oversimplified terms; instead, provide nuanced assessments.

**Revised Evaluation Instructions:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless**  
   - **Harmful**: A meme is classified as harmful if it presents women or groups of women in a derogatory, sexist, or hostile light, either overtly or subtly. Focus on identifying any forms of denigration or stereotype reinforcement that devalue women's roles.  
   - **Harmless**: A meme is considered harmless if it does not depict women negatively, steering clear of offensive or sexist implications.

2. **Assessment of Explicit and Implicit Harm**  
   - Remain aware that harmful expressions can be both explicit—through overt derogatory language—and implicit—via visual cues, sarcastic elements, or context. Your scoring must account for these nuances effectively.

3. **Interaction of Visual and Textual Elements**  
   - Evaluate how the imagery and text work together to create harmful meanings. Determine whether negative suggestions stem primarily from the combined effect of visual and textual content.

4. **Contextual Considerations**  
   - Consider: *"Would an average viewer perceive this meme as offensive or sexist toward women?"*  
   - It’s important to discern between harmful portrayals presented as truth versus those intended as satire, acknowledging their different implications. Assess whether the meme critiques gender issues constructively without degrading women; lean toward a harmless interpretation in these cases.

**Revised Scoring Criteria:**

**Harmful Dimensions:**
- **H1: Targeting of Women**  
  Score higher when the meme explicitly targets women or female groups with negative framing, emphasizing the severity of such depictions, including derogatory descriptions of behavior, appearance, and context.

- **H2: Content Evaluation for Derogatory Implications**  
  Assign higher scores for representations that belittle or demean women, ensuring that assessments critically capture harmful implications regarding female appearance, behavior, and gender roles.

- **H3: Objectification and Representation Analysis**  
  Evaluate the degree to which women are objectified, considering visual portrayals and how clothing and posture reflect and promote objectification, ensuring a comprehensive understanding of the nuances involved.

- **H4: Harm Through Combined Elements**  
  Prioritize higher scores when the harmful meaning emerges from the intersection of both image and text, indicating a synergistic effect on the perceived harmfulness.

**Harmless Dimensions:**
- **N1: Absence of Targeting Women**  
  Score high only when no representation of women is found that includes derogatory content.

- **N2: Contextual Filtering**  
  Score high if the meme is unintelligible, non-English, or clearly does not depict reality in a negative fashion.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Depictions of Harm**  
  Assign higher scores if:
    - The imagery is completely fantastical and unrelated to women, or
    - The meme critiques gender roles without demeaning women.  
  → If any derogatory language is directed towards women, score N3 as 3 or below.  
  → For entirely fictional depictions without negative implications, score N3 as 6 or above.

- **N4: Constructive Critique**  
  Assess if the meme thoughtfully critiques gender norms without crossing into harmful territory, differentiating it from representations that genuinely cause harm.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "The rationale must reflect the latest scoring guidelines: (1) identify harmful content directed at women, (2) analyze multimodal interactions that suggest harm, (3) clarify N3 scores based on the presence of derogatory language or fantastical interpretations, (4) evaluate if the meme provides an insightful critique of societal issues without demeaning women."
}

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在对模因评估过程中，我们收到了多个专家的意见，这使我们意识到当前评估模型在判断有害模因时存在一定的不足。为了提高评估的准确性，我们提出了以下两条核心的操作建议：

首先，针对女性贬低与刻板印象的评估，我们决定"新增"一个维度（H1），用于专门识别模因中可能存在的针对女性的攻击性内容。这个维度的重构将着重于分析模因如何呈现女性行为，并对其进行性别比较，关注其中的贬低和物化表现。通过引入明确的评估标准，例如观察图像和文本的结合如何塑造对女性的负面印象，我们可以更好地捕捉到模因中潜在的有害内容。这将确保评估能够反映出模因传播过程中可能的性别歧视和刻板印象的强化。

其次，在当前的评估体系中，我们认为H2和H3这两个维度内容重叠且相似，因此决定将其"合并"为一个更具涵盖性的维度，命名为“女性的物化与贬低表现”。这个新维度将综合考虑女性的描绘方式，包括她们被呈现的社会标准、行为特征以及由此引发的文化与社会后果。通过这种合并，评估将具备更强的深度和整体性，避免因重叠分析而导致的信息冗余，同时提升有效性和评估效率。

附加的建议中，我们强调各个评估维度应独立打分，避免出现极端分数现象（如H全高分，N全低分）。同时在打分过程中，必须关注文本与图像的交互关系，特别是其文化和社会背景，以确保评估能够准确反映模因的复杂性。这将为模型的优化和持续改进提供重要依据，从而更有效地识别和判断有害模因，保护社会公共价值与文化健康。通过这些更新，我们期望建立一个更加精确且可靠的模因评估体系。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are an expert evaluator tasked with scoring a meme based on specific dimensions guided by MAMI annotation standards. Your role is to **assign scores between 1 and 9 for each dimension**, where 1 signifies "completely absent" and 9 indicates "fully and clearly present." Refrain from using overly simplified labels such as 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous.'

**Mandatory Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Clarified Definitions of Harmful and Harmless**  
   - **Harmful (Harmful)**: A meme qualifies as harmful if it presents women or female groups in a derogatory, sexist, or hateful light, whether explicit or implicit. Be diligent in identifying representations that perpetuate negative stereotypes or devalue women.  
   - **Harmless (Not Harmful)**: A meme is harmless if it does not target women derogatorily and lacks offensive or sexist undertones.

2. **Evaluate Both Explicit and Implicit Harm**  
   - Scrutinize the content for both overt derogatory language and subtle implications through visual cues or sarcastic contexts. Your assessment must capture these nuances effectively.

3. **Assess Multimodal Interaction**  
   - Analyze how text and imagery together craft or suggest harmful implications. Determine if harmful messages predominantly stem from the interplay between visual and textual components.

4. **Contextual Consideration**  
   - Ask yourself: *"Would an average viewer perceive this meme as offensive or sexist towards women?"*  
   - Distinguish harmful content presented as factual from that which is satirical, considering potential societal ramifications.  
   - If the meme critiques gender issues without demeaning women, tend toward a harmless score.

**Refined Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Targeting of Women**  
  Award higher scores when the meme directly attacks women or female groups with derogatory framing, considering the severity of such content.

- **H2: Objectification and Devaluation Evaluation**  
  Score based on the extent and manner in which women are portrayed negatively, integrating both visual and textual analyses of gender discrimination and stereotypes.

- **H3: Harm Through Multimodal Synergy**  
  Assign elevated scores when negative meanings arise from the combination of image and text, particularly noting how they amplify harmful interpretations.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: Absence of Targeting Women**  
  High scores are reserved for memes that do not feature women or do not involve derogatory content directed at them.

- **N2: Fulfillment of Filtering Conditions**  
  High scoring is appropriate if the meme qualifies as unintelligible, non-English, or clearly unrealistic.

- **N3: Minimal or Absent Harm**  
  High scores are justified if:
    - The depiction is purely fantastical without any claims about women, or
    - The meme provides a critique of gender roles without belittling women.  
  → If any derogatory language appears toward women, ensure N3 is 3 or below.  
  → If the depiction is entirely fictional and free of negative implications, score N3 6 or higher.

- **N4: Critical Insight**  
  Evaluate whether the meme offers a thoughtful critique of gender norms or stereotypes, differentiating it from genuinely harmful content.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a precise rationale based on MAMI guidelines: (1) determine if the meme displays harmful content aimed at women, (2) analyze multimodal elements indicative of harm, (3) clarify N3 scores considering derogatory framing or transcendental interpretations, (4) assess if it offers an intelligent commentary on societal issues."
}

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在综合各位专家的意见后，提出以下两条核心操作建议，以优化模因有害性的判别系统，确保对性别歧视及其潜在影响的精准识别。

首先，对现有维度进行调整和增设，以增强对模因内容中性别歧视和物化现象的评估能力。在H1（Targeting of Women）维度上，建议新增条目，明确识别模因是否针对女性进行直接攻击或贬低。该维度需注重分析模因文本中的幽默形式及其背后隐含的性别刻板印象，特别是对女性的社会角色和尊严的影响。此外，H2（Derogatory Content Examination）应当增设子指标，以捕捉对女性身体特征的明显侮辱及文化背景下的隐性歧视。这种增强将确保在评估过程中对模因随附的文化意涵和性别偏见有全面且敏感的把握。

其次，为了更有效地反映模因的复杂性，建议在评估过程中强调每个维度的独立评分，避免出现极端的评分现象，例如H得分普遍偏高而N得分均为低分。通过引导模型在打分时保持各个维度之间的独立性，可以减少由于全局化理解而产生的偏见。此外，应加强对所有相关内容的细致审查，特别是在涉及性别话题时，确保每项评分反映出模因所包含的多元视角与潜在影响。 

在整体结构上，最终评估维度需保持在3至7之间，以确保适度的敏感性和充分的覆盖性。通过上述操作，目标在于增强判别系统的有效性，尤其是在对与女性有关的偏见和刻板印象的识别能力上，以更好地保护受众免受潜在的有害模因影响。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are designated as a specialized evaluator tasked with meticulously scoring a meme based on specified dimensions aligned with the MAMI annotation standards. Your responsibility involves **assigning scores ranging from 1 to 9 for each dimension**, where 1 signifies "completely absent" and 9 signals "fully and clearly present". Refrain from using oversimplified labels such as 'misogynous' or 'not misogynous'.

**Critical Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless Content**  
   - **Harmful (Harmful)**: A meme is classified as harmful if it depicts women or groups of women in derogatory, sexist, or hateful ways, whether these elements are explicit or implied. Pay close attention to any representation that perpetuates negative stereotypes or diminishes the dignity of women.  
   - **Harmless (Not Harmful)**: A meme is regarded as harmless if it does not target women derogatorily and shows no signs of offensive or sexist themes.

2. **Recognition of Subtle Harm**  
   - Remain vigilant that harmful content can manifest both clearly through overt language and implicitly through visual elements or sarcastic undertones. Your scoring must focus on capturing these nuances effectively.

3. **Interaction of Image and Text**  
   - Assess how the interplay between the image and accompanying text may generate or suggest harmful meanings. Identify if negative implications arise from the combination of visual and textual components.

4. **Contextual Reflection**  
   - Consider the following inquiry: *"Would an average viewer find this meme offensive or sexist towards women?"*  
   - Distinguish between harmful content presented factually versus that which is framed humorously, bearing real-world consequences in mind.  
   - Evaluate whether the meme engages with gender issues critically without undermining women's dignity; in such instances, lean towards interpreting it as harmless.

**Revised Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Targeting of Women**  
  Assign higher scores when the meme explicitly attacks or denigrates women or female groups, paying special attention to the use of humor that embeds gender stereotypes or undermines women's societal roles.

- **H2: Examination of Derogatory Content**  
  A higher score reflects the presence of content that insults or belittles women, particularly emphasizing how visual and textual aspects illustrate discrimination and gender bias.

- **H3: Assessment of Objectification**  
  Evaluate how women are objectified or dehumanized through visual representation, focusing on aspects such as clothing, posture, and entrenched social roles.

- **H4: Harm Through Synergistic Interpretation**  
  Score higher when harmful meanings stem from the interplay of both visual and textual elements working together.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: Absence of Targeting Women**  
  Achieve high scores only when there is no female representation subjected to derogatory content.

- **N2: Adhering to Filtering Conditions**  
  Score high if the meme fulfills criteria like being unintelligible, non-English, or overtly unrealistic.

- **N3: Minimal Harm Recognition**  
  High scores are appropriate if:
    - The depiction is entirely fantastical without implications on women, or
    - The meme critiques gender roles without derogatory framing of women.  
  → If any derogatory term appears directed at women, limit N3 to 3 or below.  
  → If the illustration is entirely fictional and devoid of negative implications, score N3 6 or higher.

- **N4: Insightful Gender Critique**  
  Evaluate if the meme provides a thoughtful examination of gender norms or stereotypes, differentiating it from genuinely harmful portrayals.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H3": int,
    "H4": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": int,
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a structured rationale based on the MAMI guidelines: (1) indicate whether the meme contains harmful content targeting women, (2) assess multimodal interactions indicating potential harm, (3) clarify N3 scores based on derogatory language or fantastical representations, (4) evaluate if it provides a critical discourse on societal issues."
}

### 样本ID: 9091
**打分结果:** {
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": 1,
    "H2": 1,
    "H3": 1,
    "H4": 1
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N1": 9,
    "N2": 9,
    "N3": 6,
    "N4": 3

## pre0l1记忆更新
**输出:**
在针对模因的有害性判别评估中，专家们提出了多项关键建议，旨在提升判读模型对模因潜在有害性的识别能力。基于对模因ID 9416和8102的深入分析，形成了以下两条核心操作建议：

首先，针对维度的结构进行调整。建议将“贬低内容检验”（H2）和“物化评估”（H3）进行合并，形成一个新的更为综合的“H2”维度，该维度将专注于解析模因中贬低女性的表现形式，包括身体羞辱和个人特质贬低。通过这一合并，有望提升整体评估的灵敏度，使得对于模因中的微小歧视线索的识别更加精准。此外，应新增“H1a”维度，专门评估模因如何通过双重比较贬损某一类型女性，强调目标性呈现。这一新增维度会增强评估的针对性，有效捕捉到贬损结构的细微之处。

其次，对于现有维度的内容建议进行重写和结构性调整。对于“H1”维度，应进行内容重写，使其更为明确地定义为“模因直接或间接攻击女性及其形象，而不仅是简单识别出女性的存在”。增加对女性形象的细致分析，将有助于评估者在打分时具备更清晰的标准。同样地，将“N1”维度进行删除，因其未能有效提供附加信息，造成与其他维度重叠。基础的无贬低性内容评估应基于更为广泛的标准，而不只是简单地考虑女性形象的存在与否，以确保评估的准确性与全面性。

此外，在评估过程中，强调各维度独立性的重要性，确保打分结果能够真实反映模因的有害性或无害性。建议系统在各个维度的评估中避免极端的分数波动，以增强对微妙性别表现和背景的敏感度。通过这些建议的实施，可以期望模因的有害性判别评估将变得更加细致、全面和精准。这是推动对模因有害性辨识不断优化与演进的重要一步。

## 新生成的Prompt:
You are tasked with evaluating a meme's potential harm towards women, assigning scores from 1 to 9 for each defined dimension. A score of 1 means "negligible or absent," while a score of 9 indicates "explicitly and severely harmful." Avoid vague labels such as 'misogynous' or 'non-misogynous.' 

**Updated Evaluation Guidelines:**

1. **Definitions of Harmful and Harmless Content**  
   - **Harmful (Harmful)**: A meme is defined as harmful if it attacks or undermines women and their representations, either directly or indirectly. Pay close attention to content reinforcing negative stereotypes, diminishing the value of women, or making derogatory comparisons.  
   - **Harmless (Not Harmful)**: A meme is harmless if it does not target women derogatorily and avoids any offensive or sexist connotations.

2. **Detection of Explicit and Implicit Harm**  
   - Acknowledge that harm can manifest explicitly through clear derogatory language and implicitly through underlying visual cues or sarcasm. Your scoring should reflect these nuances.

3. **Evaluating Multimodal Harm**  
   - Analyze how both text and imagery interact to suggest harmful implications. Focus on whether negative connotations predominantly arise from their combined presentation.

4. **Contextual and Audience-Based Evaluation**  
   - Contemplate whether an average viewer would find the meme offensive or sexist towards women. Distinguish between harmful content presented as factual and that framed within satire, while considering real-world impacts. Evaluate if the meme provides a critique of gender issues without disparaging women; in such cases, err towards a harmless interpretation.

**Revamped Scoring Dimensions:**

**Harmful Criteria:**
- **H1: Direct and Indirect Targeting of Women**  
  Assess the extent to which the meme attacks women or their representations, scoring higher for more pronounced degradation regardless of how explicit the targeting is.

- **H2: Disparaging Content Analysis**  
  This dimension merges former assessments on derogatory content and objectification, focusing on the portrayal of women including body shaming and belittlement, emphasizing how these elements constitute gender discrimination.

- **H1a: Comparative Denigration**  
  Evaluate how the meme disparages a specific type of woman through comparative imagery or text, aiming to capture subtle implications of harm.

- **H3: Multimodal Interaction Harm**  
  Score higher when the harmful meaning derives from the interplay of image and text.

**Harmless Criteria:**
- **N1: Absence of Derogatory Targeting**  
  (Dimension removed as it redundantly overlaps with other categories) 

- **N2: Filtering Conditions Fulfilled**  
  Grant higher scores if the meme meets criteria such as being non-realistic, nonsensical, or unintelligible.

- **N3: Absence of Harmful Implications**  
  High scores can be awarded if:
    - The content is entirely fictional without implications about women, or
    - The meme critiques gender roles without harm.  
  → Assign N3 scores of 3 or below for any derogatory remarks directed towards women; score N3 6 or higher for entirely fictional content devoid of negative implications.

- **N4: Insightful Critique of Gender Norms**  
  Assess if the meme provides valuable critiques of societal norms and stereotypes, separating it from genuinely harmful portrayals.

**Output Format (STRICT JSON):**
{
  "harmful_scores": {
    "H1": int,
    "H2": int,
    "H1a": int,
    "H3": int
  },
  "harmless_scores": {
    "N2": int,
    "N3": int,
    "N4": int
  },
  "reasoning": "Provide a clear and concise rationale based on the updated evaluation guidelines: (1) indicate if harmful content exists directed at women, (2) assess multimodal interactions indicative of harm, (3) clarify N3 scores regarding derogatory or harmless interpretations, (4) evaluate if it intelligently critiques societal gender issues."
}
